Let's Logic Collection ID: 632
Title: Recreation
Author: Werner Ettinger
Description: The levels in this set were collected, documented and published by Sokoplaza members. Pack author: Werner Ettinger in a combination with xht to xsb restorer program. Pack supervisor: Findus.

Published on Let's logic by Mark, with the permission of author and at the wish of Findus. At the request of author and supervisor, this collection must not be uploaded to Bjorn Kallmark's site, and must not be a part of any shareware Sokoban program.

The collection has no duplicates according to other collections, already on Let's logic site.

It is Not allowed to make this collection a part of any payable Sokoban program, such as Bjorn Kallmark's sokoban etc. You can make it a part of any freeware programs though.
